style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.4px;margin-bottom:4px\">Overlap Wt</div>'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:20px;font-weight:700;color:var(--txth)\">'+f2(overlapW,1)+'%</div>'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">port in BM names</div>'+\n    '</div>'+\n    '<div style=\"background:var(--surf);border-radius:8px;padding:10px 12px;text-align:center\">'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.4px;margin-bottom:4px\">Active Risk</div>'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:20px;font-weight:700;color:'+(activeRisk>=10?'var(--neg)':activeRisk>=5?'var(--warn)':'var(--pos)')+'\">'+f2(activeRisk,2)+'%</div>'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">tracking error</div>'+\n    '</div>'+\n  '</div>';\n}\n\n// Inline factor contribution row (expandable)\nfunction renderHoldExpandedRow(h,colCount){\n  let fc=h.factor_contr;\n  if(!fc||!Object.keys(fc).length) return'<tr class=\"hold-expand-row\" data-expand=\"'+h.t+'\"><td colspan=\"'+colCount+'\" style=\"padding:12px 16px;background:rgba(99,102,241,0.04);border-left:3px solid var(--pri)\"><span style=\"font-size:11px;color:var(--txt)\">No factor contribution data for '+h.t+'</span></td></tr>';\n  let sorted=Object.entries(fc).sort((a,b)=>Math.abs(b[1])-Math.abs(a[1]));\n  let total=sorted.reduce((s,e)=>s+e[1],0);\n  let maxAbs=Math.max(...sorted.map(e=>Math.abs(e[1])),0.01);\n  let bars=sorted.slice(0,8).map(([name,val])=>{\n    let pct=Math.round(Math.abs(val)/maxAbs*100);\n    let isPos=val>=0;\n    return'<div style=\"display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;margin-bottom:3px\">'+\n      '<span style=\"font-size:10px;color:var(--txt);width:110px;text-align:right;flex-shrink:0;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap\">'+name+'</span>'+\n      '<div style=\"flex:1;height:12px;background:var(--surf);border-radius:3px;overflow:hidden\">'+\n        '<div style=\"height:100%;width:'+pct+'%;background:'+(isPos?'rgba(16,185,129,0.5)':'rgba(239,68,68,0.4)')+';border-radius:3px\"></div>'+\n      '</div>'+\n      '<span style=\"font-size:10px;font-weight:600;width:50px;color:'+(isPos?'var(--pos)':'var(--neg)')+';text-align:right\">'+(isPos?'+':'')+val.toFixed(2)+'</span>'+\n    '</div>';\n  }).join('');\n  let moreCount=sorted.length>8?sorted.length-8:0;\n  return'<tr class=\"hold-expand-row\" data-expand=\"'+h.t+'\"><td colspan=\"'+colCount+'\" style=\"padding:10px 16px 10px 24px;background:rgba(99,102,241,0.04);border-left:3px solid var(--pri)\">'+\n    '<div style=\"display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:16px;align-items:start\">'+\n      '<div>'+\n        '<div style=\"font-size:10px;font-weight:600;color:var(--txt);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.4px;margin-bottom:6px\">Factor Risk Contributions (top 8)</div>'+\n        bars+\n        (moreCount?'<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt);margin-top:2px\">+'+moreCount+' more factors</div>':'')+\n      '</div>'+\n      '<div>'+\n        '<div style=\"font-size:10px;font-weight:600;color:var(--txt);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.4px;margin-bottom:6px\">Summary</div>'+\n        '<div style=\"display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:8px\">'+\n          '<div style=\"background:var(--surf);border-radius:6px;padding:8px;text-align:center\">'+\n            '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">Net Factor</div>'+\n            '<div style=\"font-size:14px;font-weight:700;color:'+(total>=0?'var(--pos)':'var(--neg)')+'\">'+(total>=0?'+':'')+total.toFixed(2)+'%</div>'+\n          '</div>'+\n          '<div style=\"background:var(--surf);border-radius:6px;padding:8px;text-align:center\">'+\n            '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">Factors</div>'+\n            '<div style=\"font-size:14px;font-weight:700;color:var(--txth)\">'+sorted.length+'</div>'+\n          '</div>'+\n          '<div style=\"background:var(--surf);border-radius:6px;padding:8px;text-align:center\">'+\n            '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">Stock-Specific</div>'+\n            '<div style=\"font-size:14px;font-weight:700;color:var(--txth)\">'+f2(h.mcr,2)+'</div>'+\n          '</div>'+\n          '<div style=\"background:var(--surf);border-radius:6px;padding:8px;text-align:center\">'+\n            '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">Total TE%</div>'+\n            '<div style=\"font-size:14px;font-weight:700;color:'+((h.tr||0)>=0?'var(--pos)':'var(--neg)')+'\">'+fp(h.tr,1)+'%</div>'+\n          '</div>'+\n        '</div>'+\n        '<button class=\"export-btn\" style=\"margin-top:6px;font-size:10px\" onclick=\"event.stopPropagation();oSt(\\''+h.t+'\\')\">Full Detail &rarr;</button>'+\n      '</div>'+\n    '</div>'+\n  '</td></tr>';\n}\n\n// Toggle inline expansion\nfunction toggleHoldExpand(ticker,e){\n  e.stopPropagation();\n  if(_holdExpanded[ticker])delete _holdExpanded[ticker];\n  else _holdExpanded[ticker]=true;\n  renderHoldTab();\n}\n\n// Set holdings view mode\nfunction setHoldView(mode){\n  _holdView=mode;\n  _holdLoadAll=false;\n  hp=1;\n  renderHoldTab();\n}\n\n// Card view renderer\nfunction renderHoldCards(){\n  let vis=_holdLoadAll?fh:fh.slice(0,PPG*hp);\n  let maxTR=Math.max(...fh.map(h=>Math.abs(h.tr||0)),0.01);\n  return vis.map(h=>{\n    let trVal=h.tr!=null?h.tr:0;\n    let isBmOnly=(!h.p||h.p===0)&&(h.b>0);\n    let rankCol=h.r!=null?rc(h.r):'#334155';\n    let fc=h.factor_contr||{};\n    let topFactors=Object.entries(fc).sort((a,b)=>Math.abs(b[1])-Math.abs(a[1])).slice(0,3);\n    return'<div class=\"card\" style=\"padding:12px;cursor:pointer;border-left:3px solid '+(trVal>=0?'var(--pos)':'var(--neg)')+';'+(isBmOnly?'opacity:0.7':'')+'\" onclick=\"oSt(\\''+h.t+'\\')\">'+\n      '<div style=\"display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start;margin-bottom:8px\">'+\n        '<div>'+\n          '<span style=\"font-weight:700;color:var(--txth);font-size:13px\">'+h.t+'</span>'+\n          (isBmOnly?'<span style=\"background:#334155;color:#94a3b8;font-size:8px;padding:1px 4px;border-radius:3px;margin-left:4px\">BM</span>':'')+\n          (h.isNew?'<span style=\"background:#a78bfa;color:#0f172a;font-size:8px;padding:1px '<div style=\"text-align:center;background:var(--surf);border-radius:4px;padding:4px\">'+\n          '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">Port</div>'+\n          '<div style=\"height:100%;width:'+(Math.abs(trVal)/maxTR*100).toFixed(0)+'%;background:'+(trVal>=0?'var(--pos)':'var(--neg)')+';border-radius:2px;opacity:0.6\"></div>'+\n      '</div>'+\n      (h.sec?'<span class=\"chip\" style=\"font-size:9px\">'+h.sec+'</span>':'')+' '+(h.co?'<span style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">'+h.co+'</span>':'')+\n      (topFactors.length?'<div style=\"display:flex;justify-content:space-between;font-size:9px\"><span style=\"color:var(--txt)\">'+n+'</span><span style=\"font-weight:600;color:'+(v>=0?'var(--pos)':'var(--neg)')+'\">'+(v>=0?'+':'')+v.toFixed(2)+'</span></div>';}).join('')+'</div>':'')+\n    '</div>';\n  }).join('');\n}\n\nfunction applyHoldSort(){\n  if(_holdSortMode==='risk')    fh.sort((a,b)=>Math.abs(b.tr||0)-Math.abs(a.tr||0));\n  else if(_holdSortMode==='weight') fh.sort((a,b)=>Math.abs(b.p||0)-Math.abs(a.p||0));\n  else if(_holdSortMode==='rank')   fh.sort((a,b)=>(a.r!=null?a.r:99)-(b.r!=null?b.r:99));\n  else if(_holdSortMode==='name')   fh.sort((a,b)=>(a.n||'').localeCompare(b.n||''));\n}\n\nfunction setHoldSort(mode){\n  _holdSortMode=mode;\n  fh=[...ah];\n  applyHoldFilters();\n  applyHoldSort();\n  hp=1;renderHoldTab();\n}\n\nfunction rHold(){\n  // Include active holdings + material BM-only (b>0.5 or |%T|>1)\n  ah=[...cs.hold].filter(h=>h.p>0||h.b>0.5||Math.abs(h.tr||0)>1);\n  fh=[...ah];\n  hp=1;sortCol='tr';sortDir=-1;\n  _holdLoadAll=false;\n  _holdExpanded={};\n  applyHoldSort();\n  renderHoldTab();\n}\n\nfunction renderHoldTab(){\n  // Count visible columns for colspan calculation\n  let colCount=2; // ticker + name always visible\n  if(_holdColVis.sector!==false)colCount++;\n  if(_holdColVis.industry!==false)colCount++;\n  if(_holdColVis.country!==false)colCount++;\n  if(_holdColVis.port!==false)colCount++;\n  if(_holdColVis.bench!==false)colCount++;\n  if(_holdColVis.active!==false)colCount++;\n  if(_holdColVis.mcr!==false)colCount++;\n  if(_holdColVis.tr!==false)colCount++;\n  if(_holdColVis.orvq!==false)colCount+=4;\n\n  let    '<button onclick=\"setHoldView(\\'card\\')\" style=\"padding:3px onclick=\"event.stopPropagation()\"><button class=\"export-btn\" title=\"Download\" onclick=\"let dr=this.nextElementSibling;let      '</div>'+\n      '<span style=\"font-size:10px;color:var(--txt)\">Click row to expand \\u00b7 Double-click for full detail</span>'+\n    '</div>';\n\n  if(_holdView==='card'){\n    // Card view\n onclick=\"_holdLoadAll=true;renderHoldTab()\" style=\"margin-left:8px\">Show All '+fh.length+'</button>':'')+\n        '</div>'+\n      '</div>';\n    } else {\n      html+='<div class=\"pag\"><span>Showing all '+fh.length+' holdings</span><button class=\"btn btn-sec btn-sm\" onclick=\"_holdLoadAll=false;hp=1;renderHoldTab()\">Paginate</button></div>';\n    }\n  }\n\n  html+='</div>'; // close cardHoldings\n\n  // Holdings Charts\n  html+='<div class=\"grid g2\">'+\n    '<div class=\"card\"><div class=\"card-title\">Rank Distribution</div><div id=\"rankDistDiv\" '</div>';\n\n  $('tab-holdings').innerHTML=html;\n  setTimeout(function(){rRankDist();rHoldConc();},50);\n}\n\nfunction renderHoldRows(colCount){\n  let page=_holdLoadAll?fh:fh.slice((hp-1)*PPG,(hp-1)*PPG+PPG);\n  // Max %T for bar scaling\n  let maxTR=Math.max(...fh.map(h=>Math.abs(h.tr||0)),0.01);\n  return page.map(function(h){\n    let cls=activeStyle(h.a);\n    let trVal=h.tr!=null?h.tr:0;\n    let trBarW=Math.min(Math.abs(trVal)/maxTR*60,60).toFixed(0);\n    // Enhanced TE% cell with proportional mini bar\n    let trCell=(_holdColVis.tr!==false)?'<td class=\"r\" style=\"white-space:nowrap\">'+\n      '<div style=\"display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:3px;justify-content:flex-end;min-width:80px\">'+\n        '<span style=\"font-size:11px;'+(trVal>=0?'color:var(--pos)':'color:var(--neg)')+'\">'+fp(trVal,1)+'</span>'+\n        '<div style=\"width:60px;height:8px;background:rgba(51,65,85,0.4);border-radius:3px;overflow:hidden;flex-shrink:0\">'+\n          '<div style=\"height:100%;width:'+trBarW+'px;background:'+(trVal>=0?'var(--pos)':'var(--neg)')+';border-radius:3px;opacity:0.6\"></div>'+\n        '</div>'+\n      '</div></td>':'';\n    let isBmOnly=(!h.p||h.p===0)&&(h.b>0);\n    let bmBadge=isBmOnly?'<span style=\"background:#334155;color:#94a3b8;font-size:9px;padding:1px 4px;border-radius:4px;margin-left:3px\">BM</span>':'';\n    let newBadge=h.isNew?'<span style=\"background:#a78bfa;color:#0f172a;font-size:9px;padding:1px 4px;border-radius:4px;font-weight:600;margin-left:3px\">NEW</span>':'';\n    let fcBadge=h.factor_contr&&Object.keys(h.factor_contr).length?'<span style=\"background:rgba(99,102,241,.15);color:#818cf8;font-size:8px;padding:1px 3px;border-radius:3px;margin-left:3px;font-weight:600\" title=\"'+Object.keys(h.factor_contr).length+' factor contributions\">FC</span>':'';\n    let isExpanded=_holdExpanded[h.t];\n    let expandIcon=isExpanded?'\\u25b4':'\\u25be';\n    let row='<tr style=\"cursor:pointer'+(isBmOnly?';background:rgba(100,116,139,0.1)':'')+(isExpanded?';background:rgba(99,102,241,0.08)':'')+'\" style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--pri);margin-right:3px\">'+expandIcon+'</span>'+h.t+bmBadge+newBadge+fcBadge+'</td>'+\n      '<td style=\"max-width:160px;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis\">'+h.n+'</td>'+\n      (_holdColVis.sector!==false?'<td><span class=\"chip\">'+(h.sec||'\\u2014')+'</span></td>':'')+\n style=\"accent-color:var(--pri);cursor:pointer\"><span style=\"font-size:11px;color:var(--txth)\">'+c.label+'</span></label></div>').join('');\n  return'<div class=\"dl-wrap\" onclick=\"event.stopPropagation()\"><button class=\"export-btn\" title=\"Column visibility\" onclick=\"let dr=this.nextElementSibling;let was=dr.classList.contains(\\'open\\');document.querySelectorAll(\\'.dl-drop\\').forEach(m=>m.classList.remove(\\'open\\'));if(!was)dr.classList.add(\\'open\\')\">&#9881; Cols</button><div class=\"dl-drop\" style=\"min-width:155px;max-height:300px;overflow-y:auto\">'+chk+'</div></div>';\n}\n\n// Portfolio vs Benchmark summary computation\nfunction holdSummaryBar(){\n  let portHold=cs.hold.filter(h=>h.p>0&&!isCash(h));\n  let bmHold=cs.hold.filter(h=>h.b>0&&!isCash(h));\n  let portTickers=new Set(portHold.map(h=>h.t));\n  let bmTickers=new Set(bmHold.map(h=>h.t));\n  let overlap=[...portTickers].filter(t=>bmTickers.has(t)).length;\n  let overlapPct=bmTickers.size>0?(overlap/bmTickers.size*100).toFixed(0):0;\n  let totalPortW=portHold.reduce((s,h)=>s+(h.p||0),0);\n  let cashW=cs.sum.cash!=null?cs.sum.cash:cs.hold.filter(h=>isCash(h)).reduce((s,h)=>s+(h.p||0),0);\n  let activeRisk=cs.sum.te!=null?cs.sum.te:0;\n  let portCount=portHold.length;\n  let bmCount=bmTickers.size;\n  let overlapW=portHold.filter(h=>bmTickers.has(h.t)).reduce((s,h)=>s+(h.p||0),0);\n\n  return'<div style=\"display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(6,1fr);gap:8px;margin-bottom:12px\">'+\n    '<div style=\"background:var(--surf);border-radius:8px;padding:10px 12px;text-align:center\">'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.4px;margin-bottom:4px\">Port Holdings</div>'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:20px;font-weight:700;color:var(--txth)\">'+portCount+'</div>'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">vs '+bmCount+' BM</div>'+\n    '</div>'+\n    '<div style=\"background:var(--surf);border-radius:8px;padding:10px 12px;text-align:center\">'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.4px;margin-bottom:4px\">Invested</div>'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:20px;font-weight:700;color:var(--txth)\">'+f2(totalPortW,1)+'%</div>'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">equity weight</div>'+\n    '</div>'+\n    '<div style=\"background:var(--surf);border-radius:8px;padding:10px 12px;text-align:center\">'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.4px;margin-bottom:4px\">Cash</div>'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:20px;font-weight:700;color:'+(cashW>5?'var(--warn)':'var(--txth)')+'\">'+f2(cashW,1)+'%</div>'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">'+(cashW>5?'elevated':'normal')+'</div>'+\n    '</div>'+\n    '<div style=\"background:var(--surf);border-radius:8px;padding:10px 12px;text-align:center\">'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.4px;margin-bottom:4px\">BM Overlap</div>'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:20px;font-weight:700;color:var(--txth)\">'+overlapPct+'%</div>'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">'+overlap+' of '+bmTickers.size+' names</div>'+\n    '</div>'+\n    '<div style=\"background:var(--surf);border-radius:8px;padding:10px 12px;text-align:center\">'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.4px;margin-bottom:4px\">Overlap Wt</div>'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:20px;font-weight:700;color:var(--txth)\">'+f2(overlapW,1)+'%</div>'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">port in BM names</div>'+\n    '</div>'+\n    '<div style=\"background:var(--surf);border-radius:8px;padding:10px 12px;text-align:center\">'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.4px;margin-bottom:4px\">Active Risk</div>'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:20px;font-weight:700;color:'+(activeRisk>=10?'var(--neg)':activeRisk>=5?'var(--warn)':'var(--pos)')+'\">'+f2(activeRisk,2)+'%</div>'+\n      '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">tracking error</div>'+\n    '</div>'+\n  '</div>';\n}\n\n// Inline factor contribution row (expandable)\nfunction renderHoldExpandedRow(h,colCount){\n  let fc=h.factor_contr;\n  if(!fc||!Object.keys(fc).length) return'<tr class=\"hold-expand-row\" data-expand=\"'+h.t+'\"><td colspan=\"'+colCount+'\" style=\"padding:12px 16px;background:rgba(99,102,241,0.04);border-left:3px solid var(--pri)\"><span style=\"font-size:11px;color:var(--txt)\">No factor contribution data for '+h.t+'</span></td></tr>';\n  let sorted=Object.entries(fc).sort((a,b)=>Math.abs(b[1])-Math.abs(a[1]));\n  let total=sorted.reduce((s,e)=>s+e[1],0);\n  let maxAbs=Math.max(...sorted.map(e=>Math.abs(e[1])),0.01);\n  let bars=sorted.slice(0,8).map(function(pair){\n    let name=pair[0],val=pair[1];\n    let pct=Math.round(Math.abs(val)/maxAbs*100);\n    let isPos=val>=0;\n    return'<div style=\"font-size:10px;color:var(--txt);width:110px;text-align:right;flex-shrink:0;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap\">'+name+'</span>'+\n      '<div style=\"flex:1;height:12px;background:var(--surf);border-radius:3px;overflow:hidden\">'+\n        '<div style=\"height:100%;width:'+pct+'%;background:'+(isPos?'rgba(16,185,129,0.5)':'rgba(239,68,68,0.4)')+';border-radius:3px\"></div>'+\n      '</div>'+\n      '<span style=\"font-size:10px;font-weight:600;width:50px;color:'+(isPos?'var(--pos)':'var(--neg)')+';text-align:right\">'+(isPos?'+':'')+val.toFixed(2)+'</span>'+\n    '</div>';\n  }).join('');\n  let moreCount=sorted.length>8?sorted.length-8:0;\n  return'<tr class=\"hold-expand-row\" data-expand=\"'+h.t+'\"><td colspan=\"'+colCount+'\" style=\"padding:10px 16px 10px 24px;background:rgba(99,102,241,0.04);border-left:3px solid var(--pri)\">'+\n    '<div style=\"display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:16px;align-items:start\">'+\n      '<div>'+\n        '<div (moreCount?'<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt);margin-top:2px\">+'+moreCount+' more factors</div>':'')+\n      '</div>'+\n      '<div>'+\n        '<div style=\"font-size:10px;font-weight:600;color:var(--txt);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.4px;margin-bottom:6px\">Summary</div>'+\n        '<div style=\"display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr          '<div style=\"font-size:14px;font-weight:700;color:'+(total>=0?'var(--pos)':'var(--neg)')+'\">'+(total>=0?'+':'')+total.toFixed(2)+'%</div>'+\n          '</div>'+\n          '<div style=\"background:var(--surf);border-radius:6px;padding:8px;text-align:center\">'+\n            '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">Factors</div>'+\n            '<div style=\"font-size:14px;font-weight:700;color:'+((h.tr||0)>=0?'var(--pos)':'var(--neg)')+'\">'+fp(h.tr,1)+'%</div>'+\n          '</div>'+\n        '</div>'+\n        '<button class=\"export-btn\" style=\"margin-top:6px;font-size:10px\" onclick=\"event.stopPropagation();oSt(\\''+h.t+'\\')\">Full Detail &rarr;</button>'+\n      '</div>'+\n    '</div>'+\n  '</td></tr>';\n}\n\n// Toggle inline expansion\nfunction toggleHoldExpand(ticker,e){\n  e.stopPropagation();\n  if(_holdExpanded[ticker])delete _holdExpanded[ticker];\n  else _holdExpanded[ticker]=true;\n  renderHoldTab();\n}\n\n// Set holdings view mode\nfunction setHoldView(mode){\n  _holdView=mode;\n  _holdLoadAll=false;\n  hp=1;\n  renderHoldTab();\n}\n\n// Card view renderer\nfunction renderHoldCards(){\n  let vis=_holdLoadAll?fh:fh.slice(0,PPG*hp);\n  let maxTR=Math.max(...fh.map(h=>Math.abs(h.tr||0)),0.01);\n  return vis.map(function(h){\n    let trVal=h.tr!=null?h.tr:0;\n    let isBmOnly=(!h.p||h.p===0)&&(h.b>0);\n    let rankCol=h.r!=null?rc(h.r):'#334155';\n    let fc=h.factor_contr||{};\n    let topFactors=Object.entries(fc).sort((a,b)=>Math.abs(b[1])-Math.abs(a[1])).slice(0,3);\n    return'<div class=\"card\" style=\"padding:12px;cursor:pointer;border-left:3px solid '+(trVal>=0?'var(--pos)':'var(--neg)')+';'+(isBmOnly?'opacity:0.7':'')+'\" onclick=\"oSt(\\''+h.t+'\\')\">'+\n      '<div style=\"display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start;margin-bottom:8px\">'+\n        '<div>'+\n          '<span '<div style=\"text-align:center;background:var(--surf);border-radius:4px;padding:4px\">'+\n          '<div style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">Port</div>'+\n          '<div class=\"chip\" style=\"font-size:9px\">'+h.sec+'</span>':'')+' '+(h.co?'<span style=\"font-size:9px;color:var(--txt)\">'+h.co+'</span>':'')+\n      (topFactors.length?'<div applyHoldSort(){\n  if(_holdSortMode==='risk')    fh.sort((a,b)=>Math.abs(b.tr||0)-Math.abs(a.tr||0));\n  else if(_holdSortMode==='weight') fh.sort((a,b)=>Math.abs(b.p||0)-Math.abs(a.p||0));\n  else if(_holdSortMode==='rank')   fh.sort((a,b)=>(a.r!=null?a.r:99)-(b.r!=null?b.r:99));\n  else if(_holdSortMode==='name')   fh.sort((a,b)=>(a.n||'').localeCompare(b.n||''));\n}\n\nfunction setHoldSort(mode){\n  _holdSortMode=mode;\n  fh=[...ah];\n  applyHoldFilters();\n  applyHoldSort();\n  hp=1;renderHoldTab();\n}\n\nfunction rHold(){\n  // Include active holdings + material BM-only (b>0.5 or |%T|>1)\n  ah=[...cs.hold].filter(h=>h.p>0||h.b>0.5||Math.abs(h.tr||0)>1);\n  fh=[...ah];\n  hp=1;sortCol='tr';sortDir=-1;\n  _holdLoadAll=false;\n  _holdExpanded={};\n  applyHoldSort();\n  renderHoldTab();\n}\n\nfunction renderHoldTab(){\n  // Count visible columns for colspan calculation\n  let colCount=2; // ticker + name always visible\n  if(_holdColVis.sector!==false)colCount++;\n  if(_holdColVis.industry!==false)colCount++;\n  if(_holdColVis.country!==false)colCount++;\n  if(_holdColVis.port!==false)colCount++;\n  if(_holdColVis.bench!==false)colCount++;\n  if(_holdColVis.active!==false)colCount++;\n  if(_holdColVis.mcr!==false)colCount++;\n  if(_holdColVis.tr!==false)colCount++;\n  if(_holdColVis.orvq!==false)colCount+=4;\n\n  let Immediately shows which holdings dominate risk and whether they deserve it.\n\n2. **\"Risk Budget Efficiency\" Column** -- A computed metric: `(active return attribution) / (TE contribution)`. Holdings earning more return per unit of risk show green; risk-wasters show red. Answers \"is this holding earning its risk budget?\" at a glance.\n\n3. **Holdings Comparison Mode** -- Select 2-5 holdings (checkboxes) and pop up a side-by-side comparison card: factor profiles overlaid on the same radar chart, weight history overlaid, rank trajectories. PMs could quickly compare whether to swap one holding for another.\n\n4. **\"What If\" Weight Slider** -- On the expanded row, add a slider to simulate changing a holding's weight. Show the estimated impact on portfolio TE, active weight, and factor exposures in real-time. Would make the tab actionable, not just informational.\n\n5. **Smart Alerts Row** -- A colored banner row that appears when a holding crosses a threshold (e.g., TE contribution >5%, rank deteriorated to Q5, or active weight exceeds sector peers).
